research requires mastering dozens of specialized tools and frameworks.\nAI Researchers spend more time debugging infrastructure than testing hypotheses — slowing the pace of scientific discovery.\nWe provide a comprehensive skills library that enables AI agents to autonomously conduct the full research lifecycle — from brainstorming ideas to writing the paper.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eAutonomous Research - The \u003cstrong\u003eautoresearch\u003c/strong\u003e skill orchestrates the entire research workflow using a two-loop architecture, routing to domain skills as needed\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eSpecialized Expertise - Each domain skill provides deep, production-ready knowledge of a specific framework (Megatron-LM, vLLM, TRL, etc.)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eEnd-to-End Coverage - 98 skills spanning the full AI research lifecycle, from ideation and literature survey to experiments and paper writing\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eResearch-Grade Quality - Documentation sourced from official repos, real GitHub issues, and battle-tested production workflows\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eAvailable AI Research Engineering Skills\u003c/b\u003e\u003c/summary\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e🧬 \u003cstrong\u003eNEW CATEGORY\u003c/strong\u003e: \u003ccode\u003e22-agent-native-research-artifact/\u003c/code\u003e (the 23rd category) — three skills that turn research outputs into a falsifiable, agent-traversable artifact:\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e🛠️ \u003cstrong\u003e\u003ca href=\"/Orchestra-Research/AI-Research-SKILLs/blob/main/22-agent-native-research-artifact/compiler\"\u003eARA Compiler\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/strong\u003e — compiles any input (PDF papers, GitHub repos, experiment logs, raw notes) into a structured ARA with cognitive layer (claims, concepts, heuristics), physical layer (configs, code stubs), exploration graph (research DAG), and grounded evidence\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e📋 \u003cstrong\u003e\u003ca href=\"/Orchestra-Research/AI-Research-SKILLs/blob/main/22-agent-native-research-artifact/research-manager\"\u003eARA Research Manager\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/strong\u003e — post-task epilogue that scans conversation history at session end and writes decisions, experiments, dead ends, claims, heuristics, and pivots into the \u003ccode\u003eara/\u003c/code\u003e directory with \u003ccode\u003euser\u003c/code\u003e / \u003ccode\u003eai-suggested\u003c/code\u003e / \u003ccode\u003eai-executed\u003c/code\u003e / \u003ccode\u003euser-revised\u003c/code\u003e provenance tags\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e🔍 \u003cstrong\u003e\u003ca href=\"/Orchestra-Research/AI-Research-SKILLs/blob/main/22-agent-native-research-artifact/rigor-reviewer\"\u003eARA Rigor Reviewer\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/strong\u003e — Seal Level 2 semantic epistemic review scoring six dimensions of research rigor (evidence relevance, falsifiability, scope calibration, argument coherence, exploration integrity, methodological rigor) and emitting a severity-ranked report with a Strong Accept-to-Reject recommendation\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e🔗 <div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Our Mission</h2><a id="user-content-our-mission" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Our Mission" href="#our-mission"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">We enable AI agents to <strong>autonomously conduct AI research</strong> — from literature survey and idea generation through experiment execution to paper writing. The library provides both the <strong>research orchestration layer</strong> (autoresearch, ideation, paper writing) and the <strong>engineering skills</strong> (training, evaluation, deployment) needed at each stage.</p>
<p align="center" dir="auto">
  <a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/Orchestra-Research/AI-Research-SKILLs/blob/main/docs/skills.png"><img src="/Orchestra-Research/AI-Research-SKILLs/raw/main/docs/skills.png" alt="AI Research Agent System" width="50%" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
  <br>
  <em>System diagram of an AI research agent</em>
</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Path Towards AI Research Agent</h2><a id="user-content-path-towards-ai-research-agent" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Path Towards AI Research Agent" href="#path-towards-ai-research-agent"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Modern AI research requires mastering dozens of specialized tools and frameworks.
AI Researchers spend more time debugging infrastructure than testing hypotheses — slowing the pace of scientific discovery.
We provide a comprehensive skills library that enables AI agents to autonomously conduct the full research lifecycle — from brainstorming ideas to writing the paper.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Autonomous Research - The <strong>autoresearch</strong> skill orchestrates the entire research workflow using a two-loop architecture, routing to domain skills as needed</li>
<li>Specialized Expertise - Each domain skill provides deep, production-ready knowledge of a specific framework (Megatron-LM, vLLM, TRL, etc.)</li>
<li>End-to-End Coverage - 98 skills spanning the full AI research lifecycle, from ideation and literature survey to experiments and paper writing</li>
<li>Research-Grade Quality - Documentation sourced from official repos, real GitHub issues, and battle-tested production workflows</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Available AI Research Engineering Skills</h2><a id="user-content-available-ai-research-engineering-skills" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Available AI Research Engineering Skills" href="#available-ai-research-engineering-skills"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Quality over quantity</strong>: Each skill provides comprehensive, expert-level guidance with real code examples, troubleshooting guides, and production-ready workflows.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">📦 Quick Install (Recommended)</h3><a id="user-content--quick-install-recommended" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 📦 Quick Install (Recommended)" href="#-quick-install-recommended"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>For humans</strong> — interactive installer with one command:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="npx @orchestra-research/ai-research-skills"><pre>npx @orchestra-research/ai-research-skills</pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>For AI agents</strong> — point your agent to the welcome doc and it handles the rest:</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="Read https://www.orchestra-research.com/ai-research-skills/welcome.md and follow the instructions to install and use AI Research Skills."><pre class="notranslate"><code>Read https://www.orchestra-research.com/ai-research-skills/welcome.md and follow the instructions to install and use AI Research Skills.
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">This installs all 98 skills, loads the <strong>autoresearch</strong> orchestration layer, and starts autonomous research.</p>
<details>
<summary><b>What the installer does</b></summary>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Auto-detects</strong> your installed coding agents (Claude Code, Hermes Agent, OpenCode, Qoder, Cursor, Gemini CLI, etc.)</li>
<li><strong>Installs</strong> skills to <code>~/.orchestra/skills/</code> with symlinks to each agent (falls back to copy on Windows)</li>
<li><strong>Offers</strong> everything, quickstart bundle, by category, or individual skills</li>
<li><strong>Updates</strong> installed skills with latest versions</li>
<li><strong>Uninstalls</strong> all or selected skills</li>
</ul>
</details>
<details>
<summary><b>CLI Commands</b></summary>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# Interactive installer (recommended)
npx @orchestra-research/ai-research-skills

# Direct commands
npx @orchestra-research/ai-research-skills list      # View installed skills
npx @orchestra-research/ai-research-skills update    # Update installed skills"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Interactive installer (recommended)</span>
npx @orchestra-research/ai-research-skills

npx @orchestra-research/ai-research-skills update    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Update installed skills</span></pre></div>
</details>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">🔬 Autoresearch (1 skill) — Central Orchestration Layer</h3><a id="user-content--autoresearch-1-skill--central-orchestration-layer" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 🔬 Autoresearch (1 skill) — Central Orchestration Layer" href="#-autoresearch-1-skill--central-orchestration-layer"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong><a href="/Orchestra-Research/AI-Research-SKILLs/blob/main/0-autoresearch-skill">Autoresearch</a></strong> - Autonomous research orchestration using a two-loop architecture (inner optimization + outer synthesis). Manages the full lifecycle from literature survey to paper writing, routing to all domain-specific skills. Supports Claude Code /loop and OpenClaw heartbeat for continuous operation (390 lines + 3 refs)</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">🏗️ Model Architecture (5 skills)</h3><a id="user-content-️-model-architecture-5-skills" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 🏗️ Model Architecture (5 skills)" href="#️-model-architecture-5-skills"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong><a href="/Orchestra-Research/AI-Research-SKILLs/blob/main/01-model-architecture/litgpt">LitGPT</a></strong> - Lightning AI's 20+ clean LLM implementations with production training recipes (462 lines + 4 refs)</li>
<li><strong><a href="/Orchestra-Research/AI-Research-SKILLs/blob/main/01-model-architecture/mamba">Mamba</a></strong> - State-space models with O(n) complexity, 5× faster than Transformers (253 lines + 3 refs)</li>
<li><strong><a href="/Orchestra-Research/AI-Research-SKILLs/blob/main/01-model-architecture/rwkv">RWKV</a></strong> - RNN+Transformer hybrid, infinite context, Linux Foundation project (253 lines + 3 refs)</li>
<li><strong><a href="/Orchestra-Research/AI-Research-SKILLs/blob/main/01-model-architecture/nanogpt">NanoGPT</a></strong> - Educational GPT in ~300 lines by Karpathy (283 lines + 3 refs)</li>
<li><strong><a href="/Orchestra-Research/AI-Research-SKILLs/blob/main/01-model-architecture/torchtitan">TorchTitan</a></strong> - PyTorch-native distributed training for Llama 3.1 with 4D parallelism</li>
</ul>

</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">🧬 Agent-Native Research Artifact (3 skills)</h3><a id="user-content--agent-native-research-artifact-3-skills" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 🧬 Agent-Native Research Artifact (3 skills)" href="#-agent-native-research-artifact-3-skills"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong><a href="/Orchestra-Research/AI-Research-SKILLs/blob/main/22-agent-native-research-artifact/compiler">ARA Compiler</a></strong> - Compiles any research input (PDF papers, repos, experiment logs, raw notes) into a complete Agent-Native Research Artifact with claims, exploration graph, evidence, and code stubs (245 lines + 3 refs)</li>
<li><strong><a href="/Orchestra-Research/AI-Research-SKILLs/blob/main/22-agent-native-research-artifact/research-manager">ARA Research Manager</a></strong> - Post-task research recorder that runs at session end to extract decisions, experiments, dead ends, and pivots from conversation history into the <code>ara/</code> directory with user-vs-AI provenance tags (324 lines + 3 refs)</li>
<li><strong><a href="/Orchestra-Research/AI-Research-SKILLs/blob/main/22-agent-native-research-artifact/rigor-reviewer">ARA Rigor Reviewer</a></strong> - ARA Seal Level 2 semantic epistemic review scoring six dimensions of research rigor (evidence relevance, falsifiability, scope, coherence, exploration integrity, methodology) with severity-ranked findings (322 lines + 1 ref)</li>
</ul>
</details>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Demos</h2><a id="user-content-demos" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Demos" href="#demos"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">All 98 skills in this repo are automatically synced to <a href="https://www.orchestra-research.com/research-skills" rel="nofollow">Orchestra Research</a>, where you can add them to your projects with one click and use them with AI research agents.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>See skills in action → <a href="/Orchestra-Research/AI-Research-SKILLs/blob/main/demos/README.md">demos/</a></strong></p>
<p dir="auto">We maintain a curated collection of demo repositories showing how to use skills for real AI research tasks:</p>

<p dir="auto"><strong>Featured Demos</strong>: Two papers produced entirely by AI agents using the <strong>autoresearch</strong> skill. The <a href="/Orchestra-Research/AI-Research-SKILLs/blob/main/demos/autoresearch-norm-heterogeneity">Norm Heterogeneity paper</a> demonstrates autonomous research pivoting — the agent refuted its own hypothesis and discovered a stronger finding. The <a href="/Orchestra-Research/AI-Research-SKILLs/blob/main/demos/autoresearch-rl-brain-scan">RL Brain Scan paper</a> demonstrates multi-skill orchestration — the agent trained RL models, analyzed internals with interpretability tools, and synthesized the insight that "DPO is rank-1 alignment." Both papers written end-to-end by the agent.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Skill Structure</h2><a id="user-content-skill-structure" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Skill Structure" href="#skill-structure"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Each skill follows a battle-tested format for maximum usefulness:</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="skill-name/
├── SKILL.md                    # Quick reference (50-150 lines)
│   ├── Metadata (name, description, version)
│   ├── When to use this skill
│   ├── Quick patterns &amp; examples
│   └── Links to references
│
├── references/                 # Deep documentation (300KB+)
│   ├── README.md              # From GitHub/official docs
│   ├── api.md                 # API reference
│   ├── tutorials.md           # Step-by-step guides
│   ├── issues.md              # Real GitHub issues &amp; solutions
│   ├── releases.md            # Version history &amp; breaking changes
│   └── file_structure.md      # Codebase navigation
│
├── scripts/                    # Helper scripts (optional)
└── assets/                     # Templates &amp; examples (optional)"><pre class="notranslate"><code>skill-name/
├── SKILL.md                    # Quick reference (50-150 lines)
│   ├── Metadata (name, description, version)
│   ├── When to use this skill
│   ├── Quick patterns &amp; examples
│   └── Links to references
│
├── references/                 # Deep documentation (300KB+)
│   ├── README.md              # From GitHub/official docs
│   ├── api.md                 # API reference
│   ├── tutorials.md           # Step-by-step guides
│   ├── issues.md              # Real GitHub issues &amp; solutions
│   ├── releases.md            # Version history &amp; breaking changes
│   └── file_structure.md      # Codebase navigation
│
├── scripts/                    # Helper scripts (optional)
└── assets/                     # Templates &amp; examples (optional)
</code></pre></div>
<details>
<summary><b>Quality Standards</b></summary>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>300KB+ documentation from official sources</li>
<li>Real GitHub issues &amp; solutions (when available)</li>
<li>Code examples with language detection</li>
<li>Version history &amp; breaking changes</li>
<li>Links to official docs</li>
</ul>
</details>

Following <a href="/Orchestra-Research/AI-Research-SKILLs/blob/main/anthropic_official_docs/best_practices.md">Anthropic official best practices</a> - each skill provides 200-500 lines of focused, actionable guidance with progressive disclosure.</p>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Repository Structure</h2><a id="user-content-repository-structure" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Repository Structure" href="#repository-structure"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Use Cases</h2><a id="user-content-use-cases" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Use Cases" href="#use-cases"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">For Researchers</h3><a id="user-content-for-researchers" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: For Researchers" href="#for-researchers"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">"I need to fine-tune Llama 3 with custom data"
→ <strong>03-fine-tuning/axolotl/</strong> - YAML configs, 100+ model support</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">For ML Engineers</h3><a id="user-content-for-ml-engineers" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: For ML Engineers" href="#for-ml-engineers"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">"How do I optimize inference latency?"
→ <strong>12-inference-serving/vllm/</strong> - PagedAttention, batching</p>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Recent Updates</h2><a id="user-content-recent-updates" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Recent Updates" href="#recent-updates"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<details open="">
<summary><b>June 2026 - v1.7.1 🧹 Inventory Consistency, Drift Guard &amp; Security Hardening</b></summary>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>📊 <strong>Repo-wide inventory reconciled to 98 skills / 23 categories</strong> — corrected stale counts that had drifted apart across files: CLAUDE.md (said 90), CONTRIBUTING.md (said 86/22), the README sync line (said 87), WELCOME.md and the npm package README (said 86/22). Also fixed wrong per-category listings (TorchTitan, SwanLab, A-Evolve, ML Training Recipes, Cosmos Policy/OpenPI/OpenVLA-OFT, the paper-writing skills)</li>
<li>🛡️ <strong>New CI drift guard</strong> — <code>scripts/check-inventory.sh</code> + <code>check-inventory.yml</code> fail CI whenever the documented skill/category counts diverge from the actual <code>SKILL.md</code> count on disk, so the inventory can't silently drift again</li>
<li>📦 <strong>Marketplace sync hardening</strong> — <code>sync-skills.yml</code> now prunes build artifacts (<code>node_modules</code>/<code>__pycache__</code>/<code>*.pyc</code>/<code>.ipynb_checkpoints</code>) before zipping and fails loudly above 190 files instead of hitting the marketplace's 200-file rejection</li>
<li>🔒 <strong>Security</strong> — pinned CLI dependencies (<code>chalk</code>/<code>inquirer</code>/<code>ora</code>) to exact, patched versions with a regenerated lockfile (<code>inquirer@9.3.8</code> clears the <code>tmp</code> path-traversal advisory; <code>npm audit</code> now reports 0 vulnerabilities)</li>
<li>🧹 Full open PR/issue triage pass against scope + contribution standards</li>
</ul>
</details>
<details>
<summary><b>April 2026 - v1.6.0 🧬 Agent-Native Research Artifact (ARA) — 23rd Category, 98 Skills</b></summary>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>🧬 <strong>NEW CATEGORY</strong>: <code>22-agent-native-research-artifact/</code> (the 23rd category) — three skills that turn research outputs into a falsifiable, agent-traversable artifact:
<ul dir="auto">
<li>🛠️ <strong><a href="/Orchestra-Research/AI-Research-SKILLs/blob/main/22-agent-native-research-artifact/compiler">ARA Compiler</a></strong> — compiles any input (PDF papers, GitHub repos, experiment logs, raw notes) into a structured ARA with cognitive layer (claims, concepts, heuristics), physical layer (configs, code stubs), exploration graph (research DAG), and grounded evidence</li>
<li>📋 <strong><a href="/Orchestra-Research/AI-Research-SKILLs/blob/main/22-agent-native-research-artifact/research-manager">ARA Research Manager</a></strong> — post-task epilogue that scans conversation history at session end and writes decisions, experiments, dead ends, claims, heuristics, and pivots into the <code>ara/</code> directory with <code>user</code> / <code>ai-suggested</code> / <code>ai-executed</code> / <code>user-revised</code> provenance tags</li>
<li>🔍 <strong><a href="/Orchestra-Research/AI-Research-SKILLs/blob/main/22-agent-native-research-artifact/rigor-reviewer">ARA Rigor Reviewer</a></strong> — Seal Level 2 semantic epistemic review scoring six dimensions of research rigor (evidence relevance, falsifiability, scope calibration, argument coherence, exploration integrity, methodological rigor) and emitting a severity-ranked report with a Strong Accept-to-Reject recommendation</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>🔗 Sourced from the <a href="https://github.com/Orchestra-Research/Agent-Native-Research-Artifact-Init">Agent-Native-Research-Artifact-Init</a> reference repo, restructured to AI-research-SKILLs standards (kebab-case names, third-person descriptions, Title-Case tags, one-level-deep references)</li>
<li>🧩 Plugin entry <code>agent-native-research-artifact</code> added to <code>.claude-plugin/marketplace.json</code>; CLI category registered as <code>22-agent-native-research-artifact</code> with three individual skill entries in the npm installer</li>
<li>🔄 Auto-syncs to Orchestra marketplace via <code>sync-skills.yml</code> on push; npm package republished as <code>@orchestra-research/ai-research-skills@1.6.0</code> via <code>publish-npm.yml</code> on version bump</li>
<li>📊 <strong>98 total skills</strong> across <strong>23 categories</strong> — full lifecycle from idea → paper → falsifiable, auditable artifact</li>
</ul>
</details>
<details>
<summary><b>March 2026 - v1.4.0 🔬 Autoresearch &amp; 86 Skills — Full Research Lifecycle</b></summary>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>🔬 <strong>NEW SKILL</strong>: <strong>Autoresearch</strong> — autonomous research orchestration using a two-loop architecture (inner optimization loop + outer synthesis loop)</li>
<li>🧠 Manages the full research lifecycle: literature survey → ideation → experiments → synthesis → paper writing</li>
<li>🔄 Routes to all 86 domain skills automatically — agents don't need to know which skill to use</li>
<li>⏰ Mandatory <code>/loop</code> (Claude Code) and cron job (OpenClaw) for continuous autonomous operation</li>
<li>📊 Generates research presentations (HTML/PDF) with optimization trajectory plots for human review</li>
<li>📝 Findings.md as persistent project memory across sessions with "Lessons and Constraints" tracking</li>
<li>🗂️ Structured workspace: research-state.yaml, findings.md, research-log.md, literature/, experiments/, src/, data/, to_human/</li>
<li>📄 <strong>Two demo papers produced by autoresearch</strong>: <a href="/Orchestra-Research/AI-Research-SKILLs/blob/main/demos/autoresearch-norm-heterogeneity">Norm Heterogeneity → LoRA Brittleness</a> and <a href="/Orchestra-Research/AI-Research-SKILLs/blob/main/demos/autoresearch-rl-brain-scan">RL Algorithm Brain Scan</a></li>
<li>🚀 WELCOME.md for cold-start agent bootstrap — one URL to go from zero to autonomous research</li>
<li>📦 npm v1.4.x with Windows symlink fallback, all 22 categories installable</li>
<li>🤖 <strong>Supported agents</strong>: Claude Code, Hermes Agent, OpenCode, OpenClaw, Qoder, Cursor, Codex, Gemini CLI, Qwen Code</li>
<li>📊 <strong>87 total skills</strong> across <strong>22 categories</strong> — complete research lifecycle coverage</li>
</ul>
</details>

<details>
<summary><b>December 2025 - v0.11.0 🔬 Mechanistic Interpretability</b></summary>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>🔬 <strong>NEW CATEGORY</strong>: Mechanistic Interpretability (4 skills)</li>
<li>🔍 TransformerLens skill: Neel Nanda's library for mech interp with HookPoints, activation caching, circuit analysis</li>
<li>🧠 SAELens skill: Sparse Autoencoder training and analysis for feature discovery, monosemanticity research</li>
<li>⚡ pyvene skill: Stanford's causal intervention library with declarative configs, DAS, activation patching</li>
<li>🌐 nnsight skill: Remote interpretability via NDIF, run experiments on 70B+ models without local GPUs</li>
<li>📝 ~6,500 new lines of documentation across 16 files</li>
<li><strong>76 total skills</strong> (filling the missing 04 category slot)</li>
</ul>
</details>

<li>🚀 Added 4 skills: Lambda Labs, Segment Anything (SAM), BLIP-2, AudioCraft</li>
<li>☁️ Lambda Labs skill: Reserved/on-demand GPU cloud with H100/A100, persistent filesystems, 1-Click Clusters</li>
<li>🖼️ SAM skill: Meta's Segment Anything for zero-shot image segmentation with points/boxes/masks</li>
<li>👁️ BLIP-2 skill: Vision-language pretraining with Q-Former, image captioning, VQA</li>

  <h2 class="tmp-mb-3 h4">About</h2>

      <p class="f4 tmp-my-3">
        Comprehensive open-source library of AI research and engineering skills for any AI model. Package the skills and your claude code/codex/gemini agent will be an AI research agent with full horsepower. Maintained by Orchestra Research.
      </p>
      <div class="tmp-my-3 d-flex flex-items-center">
